\"modelopt_fp4\")\n        checkpoint_save_path: Optional path to save ModelOpt checkpoint\n        device: Device to use for quantization\n    \"\"\"\n    print(\"🚀 Starting ModelOpt quantization and export workflow\")\n    print(f\"📥 Input model: {model_path}\")\n    print(f\"📤 Export directory: {export_dir}\")\n    print(f\"⚙️  Quantization method: {quantization_method}\")\n\n    # Initialize minimal distributed environment for single GPU quantization\n    if not torch.distributed.is_initialized():\n        print(\"🔧 Initializing distributed environment...\")\n        # Set up environment variables for single-process distributed\n        os.environ[\"RANK\"] = \"0\"\n        os.environ[\"WORLD_SIZE\"] = \"1\"\n        os.environ[\"MASTER_ADDR\"] = \"localhost\"\n        os.environ[\"MASTER_PORT\"] = \"12355\"  # Use a different port than tests\n        os.environ[\"LOCAL_RANK\"] = \"0\"\n\n        init_distributed_environment(\n            world_size=1,\n            rank=0,\n            local_rank=0,\n            backend=\"nccl\" if device == \"cuda\" else \"gloo\",\n        )\n        initialize_model_parallel(\n            tensor_model_parallel_size=1,\n            pipeline_model_parallel_size=1,\n        )\n\n    # Configure model loading with ModelOpt quantization and export\n    model_config = ModelConfig(\n        model_path=model_path,\n        quantization=quantization_method,  # Use unified quantization flag\n        trust_remote_code=True,\n    )\n\n    load_config = LoadConfig(\n        modelopt_checkpoint_save_path=checkpoint_save_path,\n        modelopt_export_path=export_dir,\n    )\n    device_config = DeviceConfig(device=device)\n\n    # Load and quantize the model (export happens automatically)\n    print(\"🔄 Loading and quantizing model...\")\n    model_loader = get_model_loader(load_config, model_config)\n\n    try:\n        model_loader.load_model(\n            model_config=model_config,\n            device_config=device_config,\n        )\n        print(\"✅ Model quantized successfully!\")\n\n        # Validate the export\n        if _validate_export(export_dir):\n            print(\"✅ Export validation passed!\")\n\n            info = _get_export_info(export_dir)\n            if info:\n                print(\"📋 Model info:\")\n                print(f\"   - Type: {info['model_type']}\")\n                print(f\"   - Architecture: {info['architectures']}\")\n                print(f\"   - Quantization: {info['quantization_config']}\")\n        else:\n            print(\"❌ Export validation failed!\")\n            return\n\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"❌ Quantization failed: {e}\")\n        return\n\n    print(\"\\n🎉 Workflow completed successfully!\")\n    print(f\"📁 Quantized model exported to: {export_dir}\")\n    print(\"\\n🚀 To use the exported model:\")\n    print(\n        f\"   python -m sglang.launch_server --model-path {export_dir} --quantization modelopt\"\n    )\n    print(\"\\n   # Or in Python:\")\n    print(\"   import sglang as sgl\")\n    print(f\"   llm = exported model\n        host: Host to bind the server to\n        port: Port to bind the server to\n    \"\"\"\n    print(f\"🚀 Deploying exported model from: {export_dir}\")\n\n    # Validate export first\n    if not _validate_export(export_dir):\n        print(\"❌ Invalid export directory!\")\n        return\n\n    try:\n        # Launch SGLang engine with the exported model\n        # Using generic \"modelopt\" for auto-detection of FP4/FP8\n        llm = sgl.Engine(\n            model_path=export_dir,\n            quantization=\"modelopt\",\n            host=host,\n            port=port,\n        )\n\n        print(\"✅ Model deployed successfully!\")\n        print(f\"🌐 Server running at http://{host}:{port}\")\n\n        # Example inference\n        prompts = [\"Hello, how     outputs = llm.generate(prompts, sampling_params)\n\n        for i, output in enumerate(outputs):\n            print(f\"Prompt {i+1}: {prompts[i]}\")\n            print(f\"Output: {output['text']}\")\n            print()\n\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"❌ Deployment failed: {e}\")\n\n\ndef main():\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n \"--export-dir\", required=True, help=\"Directory to export the quantized model\"\n    )\n    quantize_parser.add_argument(\n        \"--quantization-method\",\n        choices=[\"modelopt_fp8\", )\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    if args.command == \"quantize\":\n        quantize_and_export_model(\n            model_path=args.model_path,\n            export_dir=args.export_dir,\n        # Only symmetric weight quantization supported.\n        return is_w4 and weight_quant.symmetric and is_token and is_dynamic\n\n    def _get_scheme_from_parts(\n        self, weight_quant: strategy=weight_quant.strategy,\n                        is_static_input_scheme=False,\n                        input_symmetric=input_quant.symmetric,\n                    )\n                else:\n   targets of config_groups: There can be N config_groups which each\n            have a quantization scheme. If ``CompressedTensorsW8A8Fp8`` leaves the raw float32 block scales,\nDeepGEMM combines UE8M0 activation scales with float32 weight scales and emits\nNaN logits. ``process_weights_after_loading`` must requantize the weight scales\nto UE8M0 when DeepGEMM is the active runner.\n\nManual / Blackwell-only: requires SM100 + DeepGEMM (DEEPGEMM_SCALE_UE8M0).\n\"\"\"\n\nimport unittest\n\nimport torch\n\nfrom sglang.test.test_utils import CustomTestCase\n\n\nclass TestCompressedTensorsFp8BlockUE8M0(CustomTestCase):\n    @unittest.skipUnless(torch.cuda.is_available(), \"needs CUDA\")\n    def test_block_fp8_weight_scales_requantized_to_ue8m0(self):\n        from sglang.srt.layers import deep_gemm_wrapper\n\n        if not (\n            deep_gemm_wrapper.ENABLE_JIT_DEEPGEMM\n            and deep_gemm_wrapper.DEEPGEMM_SCALE_UE8M0\n        ):\n            self.skipTest(\"requires Blackwell DeepGEMM (DEEPGEMM_SCALE_UE8M0)\")\n\n        from compressed_tensors.quantization import (\n            QuantizationArgs,\n            QuantizationStrategy,\n        )\n\n        from sglang.srt.layers.quantization.compressed_tensors.schemes.compressed_tensors_w8a8_fp8 import (\n            CompressedTensorsW8A8Fp8,\n        )\n\n        torch.manual_seed(0)\n        device = \"cuda\"\n        block = [128, 128]\n        N, K = 512, 1024  # N % 64 == 0 and K % 128 == 0 -> DeepGEMM-supported shape\n\n        # A bf16 reference weight, block-quantized to fp8 + float32 block scales,\n        # exactly as a compressed-tensors `float-quantized` checkpoint stores it.\n        w_ref = torch.randn(N, K, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1\n        w_view = w_ref.float().view(N // 128, 128, K // 128, 128)\n        scale = w_view.abs().amax(dim=(1, 3)).clamp(min=1e-4) / 448.0  # (N/128, K/128)\n        w_fp8 = (w_view / scale[:, None, :, None]).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn).view(N, K)\n        w_deq = (\n            (w_fp8.float().view(N // 128, 128, K // 128, 128) * scale[:, None, :, None])\n            .view(N, K)\n            .to(torch.bfloat16)\n        )\n\n        weight_quant = QuantizationArgs(\n            num_bits=8,\n            type=\"float\",\n            strategy=QuantizationStrategy.BLOCK,\n            symmetric=True,\n            dynamic=False,\n            block_structure=block,\n        )\n        scheme = CompressedTensorsW8A8Fp8(\n            weight_quant=weight_quant, is_static_input_scheme=False\n        )\n\n        from sglang.srt.layers.quantization.fp8_utils import (\n            deepgemm_w8a8_block_fp8_linear_with_fallback,\n        )\n\n        if (\n            scheme.w8a8_block_fp8_linear\n            is not deepgemm_w8a8_block_fp8_linear_with_fallback\n        ):\n            self.skipTest(\"DeepGEMM is not the active block-FP8 runner\")\n\n        # Build the layer directly (create_weights would require an initialized\n        # tensor-parallel group); the fix lives in process_weights_after_loading.\n        layer = torch.nn.Module()\n        layer.weight = torch.nn.Parameter(w_fp8, requires_grad=False)\n        layer.weight_scale = torch.nn.Parameter(\n            scale.to(torch.float32), requires_grad=False\n        )\n        layer.orig_dtype = torch.bfloat16\n\n        scheme.process_weights_after_loading(layer)\n\n        # The fix: weight scales must be requantized to UE8M0 for the DeepGEMM runner.\n        self.assertTrue(\n            getattr(layer.weight_scale, \"format_ue8m0\", False),\n            \"block-FP8 weight scales were not requantized to UE8M0\",\n        )\n\n        x = torch.randn(8, K, device=device, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1\n        y = scheme.apply_weights(layer, x)\n\n        # Pre-fix this path produced NaN; post-fix it matches the bf16 dequant ref.\n        self.assertTrue(torch.isfinite(y).all(), \"output contains NaN/Inf\")\n        y_ref = x.float() @ w_deq.float().t()\n        rel_err = ((y.float() - y_ref).norm() / y_ref.norm()).item()\n        self.assertLess(rel_err, 0.05, f\"relative error too high: {rel_err}\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    unittest.main()","lineStart":1,"lineEnd":108,"totalLines":108,"truncated":false}},"title":"sgl-workspace/sglang/test/manual/quant/test_compressed_tensors_fp8_block_ue8m0.py","time":{"start":1784536877077,"end":1784536877081}},"id":"prt_f7eafc812001ECw5VtLz93YVk3","sessionID":"ses_0815107dfffemFELmrJ7gJG87g","messageID":"msg_f7eafc592001apMn4E1j1jyE2k"}}
